<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:peul.html>peul</a> (48691)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>From</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch"><a href = vnd.unilang:middle.html>Middle</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dutch.html>Dutch</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:pole.html>pole</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>This</a> etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:incomplete.html>incomplete</a>. <a href = vnd.unilang:you.html>You</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:can.html>can</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:help.html>help</a> Wiktionary <a href = vnd.unilang:by.html>by</a> elaborating <a href = vnd.unilang:on.html>on</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> origins <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:this.html>this</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:term.html>term</a>.</i></span>
</p>

***phat.html

<p><a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>The</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:term.html>term</a> derives <a href = vnd.unilang:from.html>from</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:african.html>African</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:american.html>American</a> Vernacular <a href = vnd.unilang:english.html>English</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:as.html>as</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:a.html>a</a> deliberate misspelling <a href = vnd.unilang:of.html>of</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:the.html>the</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:word.html>word</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:fat.html>fat</a></i>.
</p>
